Title: TWG XLIV - Narwhal's Party - D4
Post by: AngryNarwhal on January 16, 2014, 04:40:36 AM
a long, long time ago, in a galaxy far, far away...
life was born. Since then, a lot has changed.

in fact it's been quite a long time since then. Not many people keep track of time these days, much less years. Not much reason to when any year is as good as the next. Not like you're going to die of old age, like some kind of barbarian. Time is pretty meaningless when you're immortal. 
Historians estimate it's been like, a million years since the nuclear age. Whatever. Who cares. Historians are mostly squares. I hear there's a killer party going down round Narwhal's place. It's been going for something approximating two centuries, according to him. Dat life of leisure right? the band is supposed to be killer. 

And now you're at the party. This is the craziest party that could ever be.
Don't turn on the lights 'cause I don't wanna see. the radio is blastin', someone's knockin' at the door
I'm lookin' at my girlfriend - she's passed out on the floor.

Oshit wait. She's dead. Like for real guys shit we got some shit here. Momma told me not to come.
What do we even do?!? We don't have police. This society is fucking utopian. Last time someone died is when that
dumbass Dr. Wagon went spacediving without a backup plan. What was that, eighteen hundred cycles ago? I'd almost forgotten his name.

Anyway. There's really only one course of action open to us. We have to find out who is responsible for this. We have to bring these PARTY POOPERS to justice. And we all know there's also only one way to do that.

Blood. 

the players.
1. lymric
2. yeagz
3. iron
4. eep
5. liftedpixel D3
6. adderallforall D2
7. deathbutt N1
8. trientalis
9. swoopdoggydog D1
10. xazarus
11. matt miller / guy


For the newbies' sake I will try and be thorough about these here rules.

1. I am the rules
2. Do not under any circumstances communicate with any player about the game outside of the game thread unless your PM explicitily states that you may do so. you may not "quote" PMs.
3. No death posts, no nights posts.
4. Vote by putting a name in bold. you may change your vote unlimited times until the day ends.
5. Majority rules the lynch at day's end. Ties will be broken in mysterious ways that only I understand (I promise there are rules about it, you just don't get to know.)
6. Inactive players suck and they aren't allowed.
7. Endgame occurs when either the PARTY POOPERS are all dead or the PARTY POOPERS outnumber the innocent.
8. Avatars are required. Don't change your username mid game (we're stuck with matt miller for the duration.)
9. Submit night actions no later than 24 hours after nightfall.
10. Any questions or confusion should be directed to me privately.
11. Do not edit your posts for any reason.

Once again I want to say that this game is fairly experimental, and balance is not guaranteed at all. This is also my first time hosting. I apologize ahead of time if it ends up being a shitstorm.

I made an example.

With 7 humans + 2 wolves:
(click to show/hide)
[a, b, c, d, e, f, g, h, i]

B and F are wolves (rolled randomly)

Adderrall version:

D1: Lynch a and B
NK C

D2: Lynch D and E
NK G

D3: Lynch F and H, human victory


Devil's Advocate version:
D1: Lynch a
NK C

D2: Lynch B
NK D

D3: Lynch E
NK G

D4: Lynch F, human victory





With 6 humans + 2 wolves:
(click to show/hide)
[a, b, c, d, e, f, g, h]

B and F are wolves (rolled randomly)

Adderrall version:
D1: Lynch a and B
NK C

D2: Lynch D and E
NK G, wolf victory


Devil's Advocate version:
D1: Lynch a
NK C

D2: Lynch B
NK D

D3: Lynch E
NK G, wolf victory

in both trials, the results were the same between the adderall treatment and the devil's advocate treatment.

So, if one set of trials can be believed, the numbers are no different between multiple lynches and one lynch. That would mean it's all up to the psychological factors, such as human ability to discern wolves and wolvish ability to snipe humans.

Also roles: More roles will probably die in Adderall's version. the math for hitting a role is about the same as the math for hitting a wolf, except NK's can kill roles.

Title: Re: TWG XLIV - Narwhal's Party
Post by: eep on January 18, 2014, 11:05:25 AM
Anywho, since no one has partied until 7 AM on a Saturday, it's time for eep's generalized theory on wolves! I've gone back and looked through the thread and I recommend that other players do as well, lest they find they were misdirected. the truest form of sky is le ciel, n'est pas? :winky:

But enough dawdling. Let us commence.

  • Humans are apt to display a certain sort of confidence in their judgments, especially early in the game, that wolves tend not to.
This is not specifically my observation, but it is a rather well-put one that a very skillful player said in a game on a different board some time ago. There are exceptions to this, of course; some humans are just naturally more passive, humans with roles are more likely to try to hide under the radar, etc. But, in a general sense, wolves are the players who prefer to lay low until pressure is put on them.

For this reason, Iron is actually pretty unlikely to be a wolf, and guy's comparative suspicion on me and Iron just for casting votes based on some loose, but not insignificant reasoning, is actually pretty strange.
  • Wolves need to keep track of a lot of lies in order to play well. This means that sometimes they slip up and contradict themselves.
Again, it's hard to tell exactly when this is happening, but it is something that is worth keeping an eye out for. Possible example that popped out for me when I went back through the thread include:

  • Wolves often perceive attention on them as greater than it actually is.
This should be a given. Because, in most cases, a wolf's win condition depends more on their staying alive than a human's depends on their staying alive, they will often have a heightened sensitivity to any attention put on them. Case in point is Lymric, who has never had the largest number of votes on him, but has claimed that he was being persecuted (http://mysticboards.us/forums/index.php/topic,1133.75/msg,50900.html). And yet, when he posted that, he was part of a three-way tie between me, himself, and guy. He had guy coming to his defense, and while I was arguing against guy's purposeful obfuscation of my and iron's votes, I was not doing anything in particular to persecute lymric, nor has lymric ever been the most strongly targeted player in this game. He has always had the power to put the majority of the votes on a different player, though he chose not to do so with guy for quite some time. That he, and guy, would perceive two votes on lymric as worthy of immediate quenching, is in and of itself worthy of examination.

  • Wolves are more likely to cast wishy-washy or unhelpful votes.
Case in point, again, is Lymric. He has, thus far, only cast votes for people who have cast votes for him, and switched from that very quickly, as if being suspicious of him is something suspicious in and of itself (it's not). Furthermore, he states that he has no real reason for voting the people he's voted for, and essentially claims that I'm a worthy lynch because, well, really anyone is at this point in the game:

Quote from: Lymric on January 17, 2014, 04:32:31 PM
Sure, someone has to be the D1 lynch, but if it could be me, why not you, eep, or Iron, or matt miller, or guy (yes I know..),  or anyone for that matter. If you want to lynch me D1, do it, but like, don't lynch me (or anyone) and say that you've  got any evidence on anyone about anything because actually zero things have happened, so were all just throwing votes around pretty much.

I guess what im trying to say is my vote for Iron and then eep held no merit, and I don't think any vote does until some actual evidence has been found

So basically, as far as he's concerned, there's no real reason not to lynch him, but lynching him is exactly the same as lynching whoever else because meh whatever.

This rules out the possibility of his being a vanilla, for instance, which would suggest that he is either a wolf or a role. But the fact that he is willing to die, as long as the person voting him doesn't claim they have evidence, suggests that he is not a role either. So what does that leave?

the room is in shambles. Guy and eep's battle of wits has dissolved into fisticuffs. They've knocked over the chocolate fountain and the ice sculpture of Princess Jasmine. Adderall is huddled in the corner mumbling about work in the morning. Xazarus is in tears over deathbutt's ankle. Swoop and Yeagz sit in chairs facing each other, eyes wide, unblinking. Iron watches intently. Finally, yeagz loses the staring contest.

"It's not fair, Lymric splashed vodka in my eye!" He protests. Lymric throws and orange at his head. the arguing continues.

Everyone is thirsty for revenge but everyone, especially guy, is too much of a giant sissy pants to do anything about it.

"Why don't we just kill them both?" Adderallforall suggests; guy nearly faints at the suggestion. Finally, when they've resolved the only thing to do is to have the two fight to the death using party favors, Narwhal reappears. the huge, gleaming tusk that has been surgically implanted in his shoulder sometime between now and his one thousandth post dominates the room and the attention of everyone in it. It shines like backlit silver. Eep once again starts to explain, but he silences her with a wave.

"I understanding we're having some disgreement as to which of these fine gentlemen is the beer pong champion of the week??" He croons. Eep is about to say no, the situation is much more serious than that, but he pokes her in the belly button.

"Now give me a piece of paper here and I'll see if I can work this out."

a sleek, spotless white android appears out of nowhere, notepad and spacepen in hand.
For several minutes Narwhal fusses with the paper, scratching out this, drawing large circles around that. He won't let anyone look over his shoulder. He asks yeagz for the derivitave of 2sinx^(2x), who knows it off the top of his head. the android brings him three more drinks; two gin and tonics and a shot of fireball. He scribbles out a few things. Finally, with a triumphant grunt, he stands up. He turns the paper around.

All he has written on the paper is "6 x 9 = 42"

"Party foul dude. you gotta leave." He makes his hand into a gun shape and points at Swoop.
"Bang."
Swoop hangs his head, turns around, and lets the doors close behind him forever.

Yeagz and eep sit in the middle of the room, holding each other, crying. the rest of you disperse, wandering into other rooms and other parts of the party. the bar in this room has run dry. you needed to clear your head, anyway.

Get those night action PMs in ASAP, preferably before 24 hours have passed.

Congrats guys, you just participated in the longest D1 ever. Also we did this which is sort of neat.

(http://gyazo.com/5eee63d1a6887f7fd9e3f9e3c7fa41fe.png)

Title: Re: TWG XLIV - Narwhal's Party
Post by: AngryNarwhal on January 22, 2014, 02:09:59 PM
the group reforms like the birth of a star - particles attract each other until their combined mass creates a burning hot superpressure. As the arrival of friends slows to a trickle, then dwindles to a stop, one question is on everyone's mind; "Where is deathbutt?

Search parties are formed and fan out. Everyone holds hands and walks in a long line. Eventually, deathbutt's remains are discovered shoved in a pantry on the sixth floor. Signs of a brutal struggle are evident: streaks blood on the walls, brokendishes in open cupboards, chocolate pudding on the floor. Extensive interrogation of the caterer turns out no useful information other than who's raw dogging who on his staff.
After a snack of deep fired calamari, you are all forced to come to terms with the fact that this nightmare is not yet over, and there is work yet to be done before you can go back to enjoying unlimited jell-o shots and rum and coke Popsicles.   

Deathbutt's butt is dead. Day 2 begins.
If no one raises any concerns about end date in the next 24 hours, D2 will end at 10:59 pm on 1/27

Title: Re: TWG XLIV - Narwhal's Party - D2
Post by: AngryNarwhal on January 23, 2014, 09:26:43 PM
Quote from: xazarus on January 23, 2014, 08:47:22 PM
I might need a clarification of the rules here, but
Quote from: AngryNarwhal on January 16, 2014, 04:40:36 AM
7. Endgame occurs when either the PARTY POOPERS are all dead or the PARTY POOPERS outnumber the innocent.
If the party poopers outnumber the innocent, then the implication is that you might as well end the game there, because they could just all announce their pooper-nesss and openly lynch all the humans.

But a bunch of people here are talking as if the last human or two who are outnumbered by wolves obviously win the technicality lottery because they won't die until the second after "endgame".  Do you guys really think "you win iff you're alive at endgame" implies a loophole?  So none of the "third party" humans technically need to kill any wolves?  Because I think it would make a lot more sense for all the non-exclusive third-party humans to team up and kill the wolves, and then we could all win, and not on a technicality.
Hopefully I can clarify this without confirming anything.

in a typical TWG game, the game is over exclusively when one team has killed the entirety of the other. However, much like in football, where you can use the victory formation to run off the clock without running a legitimate play, at a point where wolf numbers equal human, it is assumed that they will lynch and NK the remaining humans that are completely powerless to stop it, assuming ties go in wolf favor, simply to spare everyone wasting time.

This is not the case in this game. the game will simply be over at that point, without assuming any moves on the wolve's part. I chose my wording in describing "endgame" conditions carefully in an attempt to make that distinction.

I do not publicly confirm that the wolf win condition is to have the same number of living players as the human team. Nor do I publicly confirm that humans alive at that point could be eligible to win, though clearly I have taken care to leave that possibility open.

Privately, everyone's PM stated their win conditions, hopefully in a clear manner, so refer to that if you have further confusion. Once again I chose the wording for win conditions carefully, so keep in mind that every requirement for win conditions has been stated in your PM. in other words, IF your PM does NOT say "All wolves must be dead at endgame for you to win" then that is not the case; I didn't just forget to mention it.

Title: Re: TWG XLIV - Narwhal's Party - D2
Post by: AngryNarwhal on January 29, 2014, 10:06:50 PM
you all wake up to find AngryNarwhal towering over you. Collectively. He's somehow managing to be really tall at the moment. It's probably home field advantage.

"I heard some crazy nasty shit has been going down with you guys and I'm not happy about it. you all are invited to this party CONDITIONALLY, and if you're not cool you're out! Now Deathbutt is going to be the LAST CASUALTY, you got that?"

the crows mumbles uncomfortably. Lymric scratches his nose awkwardly. Realizing how poorly you have handled the situation, everyone feels pretty bad about what happened to adderall, but no one wants to get kicked out of the party, either. There is a lot more fondue to eat and a lot more belly button shots to be shooted. Plus this band is totally radical.

Finally, an anonymous voice speaks up.
"So uhhhhhh....about last night...."
When Narwhal finds out, he's pretty pissed. He's so pissed he drops his drink. He's so pissed a girl in the other room shreiks. He makes an announcement on the PA and pretty soon, those two guys who dragged her off dragged her back in, though now they're dressed as two of the Marx brothers. Weirdly though you can't quite pin down which two.

Anyway Narwhal bends down and listens to her breath.
"Seriously you guys this was my favorite friggen sister. the fuck is wrong with you guys. you're lucky though, she's only mostly dead."
He slips a large chocolate coated pill into her mouth.
"She'll wake up soon. She'll be pretty weak, so you fuckers give her her space, you hear?"

As he says this he presses a button on his incredibly futuristic supersmart armband with holographic display and a prism of light springs up around Adderall4all's unconscious body. It looks like a forcefield straight outta Star Trek.

"No more bullshit. I'm going to go get some shrimp cocktails."
 
D3 begins. None deceased overnight. Adderall4all is pseudoalive.

Post by: AngryNarwhal on February 10, 2014, 01:12:25 AM
Fuck it. you guys aren't going to change your minds about iron.

you guys lynch Iron. Game over. Endgame condition met: All Party Poopers have been exterminated.

the WINNERS: Lymric, eep, yeagz, Trientalis, xazarus


Before the reveal, a few words.
I want to apologize to the Party Poopers. I knew that they were at a disadvantage from the beginning, due to the unique mechanic I set up for them. I tried to make up for it by giving Innocent Party Goers less and less incentive to look out for the human team.
This being my first game, however, I made a number of mistakes. I severely, grossly underestimated epp/yeagz. I honestly don't even know what I was thinking. Because no single wolf was responsible for the NK, I ended up letting yeagz completely dominate them. That system also needed to be thought out a bit more, obviously.
the balance was pretty shitty. My bad. I hope you guys had fun regardless. It was fun to watch. Except for the parts where people used the logic "the game can't possibly be that badly balanced, so that can't be true." It WAS that bad. Embarrassing.

the concept of the game was to break down the entire idea of human team vs wolf team. It didn't make any sense to me, from a story telling perspective, that a vanilla would be willing to sacrifice themselves on D1 for the team. I wanted to bring the game closer to real human behavior, and that meant putting the individual over the team, in my head. Conceptually, I think the game was a magnificent success and I'm very proud.  I loved when you guys brushed on this stuff, like eep/yeagz possibly playing both sides, like the point where you threw around the idea of working with the wolves to basically choose who was alive at endgame. I think there were a few more similar things. That stuff was awesome and exactly what I was aiming for.

Anyway. the deets. Sorry for the annoying formatting, copy-paste from notepad has it's downsides.

- you can communicate with eep privately.
- eep is definitely an INNOCENT PARTY GOER, I promise.
- you win if and only if both you and eep are alive at endgame. 


Lymric: Idealist
(click to show/hide)
you are Lymric
Fucked up names we give our children, right?

you are an INNOCENT PARTY GOER. you are also an IDEALIST. you are certainly all in favor of bringing these horrible PARTY POOPERS to justice, but we don't live in an eye-for-an-eye world here. Killing them won't bring whats-her-name back. Murder is the greatest crime imaginable in an immortal world. No one deserves that, and you can't allow it, if it's within your power to stop. Momma raised you to be the better person, now go out and show 'em how big you are.

So here's how this role works. At the end of day 1, you can choose to incarcerate the lynch victim. If you do so, the lynch candidate won't die. And the end of day 2, you can choose to either keep the D1 lynch candidate in custody, or release him/her and take the new candidate into custody. People released from custody to the mob die instantly. Same crap on day 3 and etcetera. you may only have one person in custody at any given time. you may not release a person from custody before the day ends. People in custody can still post in the game thread, can speak to you and only you privately, and cannot vote for the lynch.

- you win if and only if a PARTY POOPER is in custody at the end of the game.
- you must be alive to win.
- If you die, your prisoner is released from custody and dies instantly.
- For the purposes of endgame counts, your prisoner is dead.

Title: Re: TWG XLIV - Narwhal's Party - D4
Post by: xazarus on February 10, 2014, 12:17:40 PM
First off, that's totally my bad, I had no idea it was such bad form to look at people's profiles.

Quote from: Dr. Agon on February 10, 2014, 10:43:37 AM
the wolves would be given that information as well.

it is typical that a GM gives the vanilla PM to the wolves as well so that there is not a situation where that can be done.

I thought the standard was to put the vanilla PM in the first post, with the rules, so everybody *knew* that everybody knew the vanilla PM's wording.  I took this as an indication that the wolves *might* not know the exact name of the role.  I didn't notice that eep used IPG until Lymric said he figured something out, then I realized what he was talking about.  After that I figured the sooner you used the phrase, the more likely you were to be human (the less likely you were to be a wolf who'd figured it out).

Despite the fact that I was completely wrong, it was an exceptionally good false positive.  Eep (who vouched for yeagz and guy), Lymric (clearly caught it even though he didn't actually say it), then adderall.  Three days later trient and then pixel both said it, so I figured it was just widespread enough that it wasn't a useful indicator any more.  Also everybody told me that I was wrong, because I technically was.  But *every* living human was identified by it before *any* wolf was.  I'm wondering whether there was just a difference in interest because the wolves *knew* it wasn't a human shibboleth and some of the humans thought it might be.

TL;DR: I over-thought the shit out of this, and I was wrong, but it all would have turned out better if I'd trusted it anyway.

Title: Re: TWG XLIV - Narwhal's Party - D4
Post by: AngryNarwhal on February 10, 2014, 11:15:40 PM
It made sense from a flavor perspective. There were only really two wolves, and if you hit one of them, I would assume the the wuss would basically assist in the block. Blocking the wuss would have not affected the NK.

Also, in the event of a three way wolf tie (which theoretically might have happened due to distrust) then the wuss would be the deciding vote, and if any wolf voted to NK any other wolf, that would have happened.

Fuck if I know what would have happened if two wolves tried to kill each other at the same time.
